Data type for a code segment. Can be a regular segment, block of code
segments, a par statement (cobegin/coend) as well as while loops and if
statements.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2840" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Seg"></a><a id="2845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2845" class="Datatype">Seg</a> <a id="2849" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2851" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2855" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="LTL._==n_"></a><a id="4509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4509" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==n_</a>        <a id="4522" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4524" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4525" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4529" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Datatype">NVar</a><a id="4533" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4535" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4538" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="4540" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4542" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="4543" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4545" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Datatype">LTL</a>     <a id="4555" class="Comment">-- Nat variable x has the value n</a>
  <a id="LTL._==b_"></a><a id="4591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4591" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==b_</a>        <a id="4604" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4606" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4607" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4609" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1082" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4615" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4617" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4619" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4620" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4622" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1082" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4628" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4630" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Datatype">LTL</a>  <a id="4637" class="Comment">-- Bool variable x has the value of y</a>
  <a id="LTL.isTrue"></a><a id="4677" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4677" class="InductiveConstructor">isTrue</a>       <a id="4690" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4692" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4693" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4693" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4695" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1082" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4701" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4703" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Datatype">LTL</a>               <a id="4723" class="Comment">-- Variable x has the value -- true</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

- to string for LTL formulae, self explanatory

## The LTL-rule data type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6632" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="LTLRule"></a><a id="6637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6637" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a> <a id="6645" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6647" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6651" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₁"></a><a id="6659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6659" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₁</a>   <a id="6666" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6672" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6637" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6689" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on first element</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₂"></a><a id="6727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6727" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₂</a>   <a id="6734" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6740" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6742" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6637" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6757" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on second element</a>

## Propositional logic representation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10308" class="Comment">-- Representation of propositional logic</a>
<a id="10349" class="Comment">-- data Props : Set where</a>
<a id="10375" class="Comment">--   T ⊥         : Props</a>
<a id="10400" class="Comment">--   _∧_ _∨_ _⇒_ : Props → Props → Props</a>
<a id="10441" class="Comment">--   p&#39;          : ℕ → Props</a>
<a id="10470" class="Comment">--   ~_          : Props → Props</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Translator

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10543" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Translator"></a><a id="10550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10550" class="Module">Translator</a> <a id="10561" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Translator for concurrent programs. Translates program representations into
transition relations (TransRel). The relations keep track of the LTL-formulas
related to the program statements of the programs.

### Actions

Data type for actions, reference to what happened when translating the program

### Hoare-style Triples

Represents transition relations, < pre > action < post >, where pre is the
precondition of the program statement, action the reference to the type of
program statement, and post the postcondition of the statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11900" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="TransRel"></a><a id="11905" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11905" class="Datatype">TransRel</a> <a id="11914" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11916" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="11920" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="TransRel.&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;"></a><a id="11928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11928" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;</a> <a id="11936" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11939" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="11942" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11944" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="11947" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11949" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10895" class="Datatype">Action</a> <a id="11958" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11960" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11961" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="11964" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="11969" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11971" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11973" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11905" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>  <a id="11983" class="Comment">-- Hoare-style Triple</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translates a program statement into the corresponding `TransRel`.
  * `l`: Program label of the program statement.
  * `Stm`: The program statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="transStm"></a><a id="12181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12181" class="Function">transStm</a> <a id="12190" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#865" class="Datatype">Label</a> <a id="12198" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12200" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2365" class="Datatype">Stm</a> <a id="12204" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11905" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

Flattens a list of lists into a single list.

Converts a list of segments and a label, representing a single block segment,
into a list of `TransRel`. The result contains the representation of the program
flow.

* `p`: Label of the parent segment.
* `List Seg`: List of all child segments.

Converts a list of segments into a single `LTL`. The list represents all child
segments initiated by a parent `par` segment. The result is an `LTL` used as a
precondition in order to allow the parent segment to be considered executed.

Helper function for translate that uses different translation approaches
depending on the type of segment to be translated.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15113" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="15117" class="Keyword">TERMINATING</a> <a id="15129" class="Symbol">#-}</a> <a id="15133" class="Comment">-- used to guarantee that there is no infinite looping</a>

  <a id="16602" class="Comment">-- Translate the if statement</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translate function that takes a program and returns a list of TransRel.
The list consists of two parts, first the statement specific translations,
the second the program flow relations between the segments.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="translate"></a><a id="16866" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#16866" class="Function">translate</a> <a id="16876" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3703" class="Record">Prog</a> <a id="16883" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16885" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.List.html#80" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="16890" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11905" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

## Rules to construct proofs

Contains rules to use when construction proofs. Also has functions to check if
rules are used legally. Used in ProofChecker

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17155" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Rules"></a><a id="17162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17162" class="Module">Rules</a> <a id="17168" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Data type for program rules, indexed with rule and `LTL`. Specifically for
proof-steps regarding the programs

                                             <a id="18059" class="Comment">-- control progression</a>
